Free Talk

Memories of Splendor from the Beam

— Yanzi

▲ Weng Shouqi's Resourcefulness in Assisting with Military Affairs

Weng Shouqi of Wujiang, styled Yinshi, achieved early success in the imperial examinations and excelled in both calligraphy and painting. During the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95, he abandoned his writing brush to join the military, serving under Wu Dacheng as a law enforcement officer and confidential secretary. The troops were stationed in Jinzhou. At that time, Wu's deputy was Song Qing, the Sichuan Provincial Commander-in-Chief, who had previously served under Feng Zicai. Song achieved remarkable military success during the Sino-French War at Liangshan, earning widespread admiration. Wu led over fifty battalions, while Song commanded twenty as his deputy. The Japanese knew of Song's skill in battle and greatly feared him. They frequently used disguised spies to infiltrate Wu's camp and gather military intelligence. One evening, under a faint crescent moon, Weng was on official business, leading over ten cavalrymen, galloping swiftly with muffled hooves. Passing a certain temple, he glimpsed slight movement in the fields. Upon closer inspection, he saw a pack of dogs running and chasing, their behavior particularly strange. He instructed his men to fire upon them. The "dogs" stood up and fled. Weng ordered his men to surround and capture them, apprehending four Japanese individuals, all clad in black and wearing face masks, disguised as dogs. They were taken back to the main camp and rigorously interrogated, revealing their secret mission, and were all executed according to the law. These Japanese spies had been entrusted with a critical task: to bury landmines in the fields to harm our troops. Had they not been discovered by Weng, the soldiers of the fifty battalions would have been reduced to ashes. At the time, people admired Weng's resourcefulness and his ability to eliminate these Japanese spies.

Do Not Remove the Weeds in the Courtyard: Jifu's Informal Talks

Don't Underestimate Apprentices

James Watt, who invented the steam engine 162 years ago, was once an apprentice. Michael Faraday, who invented the dynamo 100 years ago, was also once an apprentice. Apprentices are at the forefront of knowledge, leading the Industrial Revolution and the age of electrification.

China's hopes have always been placed on students. Initially, everyone's attention was focused on students studying abroad. When the students studying abroad lost their faith, everyone shifted their attention to university students. When the university students lost their faith, everyone shifted their attention to middle school students, and now it is gradually shifting to elementary school students. If teachers and students do not have fundamental awareness, then middle school students and elementary school students will also be disappointing.

Civilization is created by humans using their minds and hands. Those who can only use their minds but not their hands, or only their hands but not their minds, are hopeless, let alone those who love to talk emptily. If they are willing to use their hands and think with their brains, then there is hope for students studying abroad and university students. Otherwise, if they fold their hands in their sleeves and read books to death, die reading books, and die from reading books, then even middle school students and elementary school students will one day disappoint us. My suggestion for young people in science is:

1. Those who have been students should work as apprentices for a few years;

2. Those who have been apprentices should study as students for a few years.

A Record of the Patriotic Man's Embroidered Needle Affair

— Lu Shifang

Previously, I saw in the newspaper that the Japanese in our Eastern Provinces recruited the bandit leader nicknamed Little White Dragon, providing him with 4,000 rifles and 100,000 rounds of ammunition to disrupt local security, intending to use it as a pretext for prolonged occupation of Liaoning and Jilin. Little White Dragon pretended to be willing to follow orders, but after obtaining the guns and ammunition, he led his men directly to attack the Japanese, inflicting heavy casualties on them. Whether this account is a true record or a deliberately sensationalized story by the writer, a momentary gratification akin to gorging oneself at a butcher's shop, is unknown. However, people in the bandit world are mostly men of passion who still have a national consciousness and ethnic thoughts, unlike the meat-eaters who only know personal gain and do not hesitate to commit treasonous acts. This is what we can deeply believe without a doubt. As for the Japanese's cunning schemes, thinking of using bandits to undermine the security of the Northeast, this is even more within expectation, and this matter should be credible. When compared to them, the likes of Xi Zhi and Zhang Haipeng should be ashamed to death. I believe this incident is similar to the Ming Dynasty pirate Embroidered Needle's plan to defeat the Qing army, and I am following this up with an account of the Embroidered Needle affair, to shame those who willingly follow in the footsteps of Zhang Bangchang and Li Wanyong.

Embroidered Needle was none other than Wang Xing, a former subordinate of the patriotic hero Zheng Zhilong. He was born a pirate, of short stature, but resourceful and cunning. People at the time called him Embroidered Needle. After the fall of the Ming Dynasty, he gathered over a thousand men and defended Wen Village Fortress in Guangdong. A member of the Ming imperial family sought refuge in the fortress. Xing supported him as their leader, recruiting heroes from all directions. Officials and gentry who were unwilling to shave their heads all flocked to him. After the Qing army conquered Guangdong, they sent a proclamation to Wen Village Fortress, urging them to surrender. Xing replied in writing, saying, "We stubborn people are doing nothing more than trying to preserve China in one corner and maintain propriety and righteousness for centuries. We are not merely reluctant to part with these few hairs on our heads. As for the small piece of land by the sea, it was originally our property, and the previous dynasty always disregarded it. Why bother mentioning the new dynasty? If you insist on seizing it, then we stubborn people will die rather than surrender." The Qing army attacked with sharp forces. Xing knew he could not win and could not defend by force. He pretended to negotiate for peace, presenting a memorial requesting surrender. When the Qing army arrived, Xing launched a surprise attack, killing countless enemies. Later, the Qing troops came in full force to attack. Wen Village Fortress ran out of food. Xing, with a hoarse voice and exhausted strength, had no way out. He took poison and committed suicide. Before his death, he told his subordinates, "Everything I have done is to shame the Chinese subjects who have betrayed their country and served the barbarians." Alas, how heroic! Can he not be called a patriotic man?

A Letter from the Magistrate of Liaoyang County Fawning on the Japanese

— Written by Ms. Xiangzhu from Yingkou

This time, the brutal Japanese invaded and occupied our Liaoning and Jilin provinces. Everyone with blood and breath is filled with anger. The Japanese government sent the military attaché Major General Kawagishi to Liaoning and Jilin to appease the Japanese army who massacred our compatriots. When he arrived at Liaoyang County, the county magistrate, Yang Xianqing, was servile and obsequious, doing his best to ingratiate himself. However, being under the oppressive power of the brutal Japanese, it is still forgivable. Looking at the letter he sent to Kawagishi, praising his virtues and extolling his merits, one knows that his heart is dead and his blood is cold. The letter is recorded below:

Respectfully submitted. The Liaoyang region has enjoyed safety and happiness thanks to the ample assistance of the officers and soldiers of your esteemed country and your esteemed military. This is all due to the widespread imperial grace, which is revered by all. All of our officials and people express our sincere gratitude and respectfully report this. We respectfully request that the Imperial Japanese Ambassador relay this to His Majesty the Emperor, and we wish him ten thousand years, ten thousand times ten thousand years.

Respectfully submitted by Yang Xianqing, Magistrate of Liaochen County, and all the officials and people.

Soviet Russia's Film Project

— Yiwesheng

Soviet Russia recently had an educational slogan, saying, "All school teachers must be able to show movies."

Recently, a Moscow news reporter visited Comrade Senmyaski, director of the largest film trust in Soviet Russia. He recorded his conversation as follows:

"By the end of 1932, we will need 75,000 film operators. Where will these 75,000 film operators come from? This year, we have already trained 12,000 people in our technical schools. Next year, we can train 35,000 more. However, this number is still not enough. Therefore, this autumn, all teacher training classes have added a film showing subject. We plan to train 30,000 rural teachers (women) to make film showing their side business. The rural teachers of today are already too busy. Adding the time occupied by personal social activities, how can they have time for this? Will we increase their labor burden by adding this new job? No, this agency will allow them to hire three to four female farmers as assistants. They can train their assistants to help with schoolwork or show movies. This will be handled according to how much time this agency takes away from their schoolwork. On the one hand, it can also prepare a new job for these female farmers in the winter."

Regarding the issue of sound film, Senmyaski said:

"We are truly extremely behind in this. Today, there are only three sound film theaters in the entire Soviet Union. By the end of this year, it will increase to 100, and next year it will increase to 550. This speed of increase raises many technical problems. All existing machinery is extremely expensive and not perfect. Therefore, we must quickly complete a cheaper plan, which is to add sound attachments to ordinary projectors. This is cheap and easy. We are indeed behind in sound films, but at the same time, we also have inventions that are certainly very important for this technology. For example, one film can be produced in one place, while sound can be recorded at a radio station extremely far away in another place. Secondly, there are narrow and non-combustible films for mobile screenings. Thirdly, there are color films. Twenty color films should be completed next year."

Today's Poetry Selection

— Lin Liqin

I recently received the entire collection of Mr. Cao Dunyin of Chongming's Dunlu Poetry and Prose from Mr. Chen Jiequan. Opening the book is beneficial and provides material for study, which is very touching. Mr. Cao is a prominent scholar of Chongming. His morality and writing have long been admired by his fellow villagers. He especially excels at calligraphy, deeply understanding the spirit of Su Shi. His writings are mostly about managing the world and helping the people, and his poems and rhapsodies are mostly about worrying about the times. Now I extract several chapters of his poems from the collection as today's poetry selection.

The Warlord of Huanggu Village Moves the Tripod, the Nine Provinces Fracture. Heroes compete, splattering the blood of the Central Plains. Duke Sun leaps on horseback and rises in Liaodong. His demeanor is dignified, how heroic. A hundred battles at Yuguan, carrying a bow in his quiver. The armies of Hebei yield to the wind. The nine gates of the heroic capital build high banners. Riding a horse, Chang'an's aura is like a rainbow. The cavalry garrisoned in the Southern Suburbs flee west. The arrogant marshals of Heluo shake hands and carry their hands. Hua Yuan suddenly ascends to Zifan's bed. They argue over the punishment of the white horse, pushing for a covenant. The drums and bells of Shaoyang cross the river. Southern Henan and Northern Shanxi are noisy and tumultuous. The vanguard of a hundred thousand collapses at the sight of the wind. Tianjin cannot be defended, and Jizhou opens. The general commands to pull up the camp. On the Shenyang highway, cars fly. Alas, the ground of Peng's demise emits thunder. The smoke of gunpowder fills the sky, scattering flesh and bones. In the past, Zhang Liang ambushed at Bolang. Before Han's revenge was avenged, Qin was almost in danger. Now, the assassination to the death is no longer used. Who doubts who is the enemy? Alas, jackals and wolves fill the land, and tigers and leopards attack. Internal strife and dependence on each other. Contending for cities and land, killing many people. How many heroes have seen the heavens punish them? Do you not hear that Cen Peng and Lai She both died as bandits? Dying for the country is also a heroic ghost. Zhu San calls himself emperor but does not end well. The Southern Dong Shi of the Spring and Autumn Annals. Yuejing Ersan, Guan Chu North Capital. He is on the River for a long time. Domination has been promoted by the King. Save time, don't waste time. Before considering the case, clean and wash. The youth group calculates in. The southern barbarian shows and measures flat.

The towering Mount Yiwu rises ten thousand zhang high. Heroes leap on horseback, their spirit difficult to dispel. The pig of Liaodong is huge, and the Emperor of Heaven is unleashed. Beyond the border, the foals are fat, and autumn is desolate. In the jade tent, talented officials sound iron cavalry. Green forest heroes wear golden sable. Whose military might is strongest in the North and South today? Ashamed, the lamb's head goblet fills the court.

▲ Lament for Jiangnan One By Party Struggle Chaos Like Hemp. The season Han decline has overturned vehicles. Occasional speech is harsher than Qin's laws. Loud words turn against the scholars of Lu. Rivers and mountains stand tall, East and West Emperors. City and field only incite internal and external snakes. Leaving a single line of Jiangnan to live. Please put down your spears and armor and cherish the insects and sand.

The above poems mostly express the feelings of the time, but their land and affairs seem to be related to today's Japanese pirates in the Northeast and the internal peace issue. Therefore, I use Today's Poetry Selection as a heading.

Novelistic Carousal Society

A Country Bumpkin Visits Shanghai Again (14)

— Bao Tianxiao

The country bumpkin thought of a joke; it was also a person from our village, who came to Shanghai for the first time, and someone tricked him and said; "Rickshaws are also divided into three classes; sitting on the footrest is third class, sitting in the middle is second class, and sitting on the hood is first class." Our friend from the village was an honest and frugal person, and he believed it to be true. When he arrived in Shanghai, he really refused to sit in the middle of the rickshaw, but went to sit on the footrest, in order to save a few cents, which made the passers-by laugh.

Originally, the rickshaw can only be sat in the middle, and people cannot sit on the hood and footrest, so the rickshaw only has second class, and there is no first class or third class. It is exactly the opposite of the tram, the tram only has first class and third class, but no second class. Just as he was thinking about this, he couldn't help but exclaim, "Huh! Strange, strange!"

It turned out that sitting on his left, there was a friend who was unfolding a map of the Hankou flood. The flood map was all photographs taken by several charitable disaster relief workers on the spot. A prosperous and lively Hankou city had become a vast expanse of water. What the country bumpkin's eyes fell on was a picture in the flood map, showing a place where the water was slightly shallow, with several rickshaws dragging in the water. The water had submerged the wheels, and people could not sit in the middle, so they sat on the hood. The country bumpkin thought: I just said that rickshaws don't have first class, isn't this clearly sitting in first class?

"Where are you going? Don't pretend to be stupid, you want to buy chestnuts." The chestnut seller had sold all the tickets to the other guests, and stood in front of the country bumpkin to urge him to buy a ticket.

"How much does it cost to go to Meilanfang?"

"I'm asking you to buy a ticket! What Meilanfang?"

"Hey! Don't you even know Meilanfang? Even I, a country bumpkin, knows it, but you people who are always in Shanghai don't know."

"What Meilanfang or not Meilanfang? I'm asking you where you want to buy a ticket to?" At this time, the ticket seller was also confused, what kind of person is this country bumpkin after all?

"Are you going to see Meilanfang's play tonight?" A passenger next to him, seeing that he was not clear with the ticket seller, also wanted to explain for him.

"I don't watch Meilanfang's play, I want to go to Meilanfang's place. I'll buy a ticket, just buy a ticket to a place near Meilanfang, how much it should cost, it's how much it should cost."

The ticket seller still didn't understand after a long time.

"You said a place near Meilanfang! I don't even know where Meilanfang is staying this time he came to Shanghai? He just got on the bus and wanted to sit in second class. Now he wants to sit in Meilanfang's place, you sir, are really an Amulin,..."

"Not bad! Not bad! It's Amulin! I'm just looking for Amulin!" The country bumpkin rushed to say this.

Financial Standard Gold Rebounds and Rises

▲Rushing Advance, Sluggish Retreat, Stimulating the Rise of Nian Erliang The gold standard yesterday, the 11th, stopped its decline and began to rise again, but the trading still had rushed advances and sluggish retreats, with sixteen taels traded throughout the day. As a result, it stimulated a rise of twenty-two taels, which is a reversal of more than one hundred taels after a week of continuous decline. This is unpredictable. The reason for the sharp rise is probably due to the great contradictions in the silver market. Public telegrams continued to rise, while private telegrams fell, which stimulated people's emotions. It opened with a rushing advance, and various parties released rumors, intending to raise the large forward price, pretending to receive cash. The exchange bills were tight, and the large gangs resisted the short selling. Soon after, it broke through 620 taels. The market suddenly soared. Unexpectedly, the Dalian Gang and others tended to sell off, and the price fell slightly. The market was lacking in foreign exchange on Wednesday, but the opening was very weak, and it immediately turned up. Although the Dalian Gang had sell-offs, the buying momentum of Zhifengyong and others became more constant. However, the situation was still stable, hovering around 620 taels.

▲The Opening Jumped Out of the 600 Tael Mark The opening rose by 13 taels and 2 qian, to 610 taels. The large strip still rose by half a bant to 4375, and the silver price increased by 1.5 fen. However, the private telegram fell by as much as 2.75 fen, which was unexpected. There were ups and downs of 1-2 taels, from 11 taels to 09 taels. The buying momentum was very strong, and Tong Taichang, Yifeng, Hengxing, Bingxing, Zhifengyong, Hengchangyong, etc. all competed to buy, and the price rose by more than ten taels. The exchange market also showed signs of strength, with the British gold bank initially buying at 11 pence, then at 10 pence 875. The US dollar was initially at 36 yuan, then at 35 yuan 75, and at 9:20 it rose to 24 taels. However, Yuanxingyong and Tong Taichang sold off, and the price immediately fell by 4-5 taels. The British gold quote remained unchanged, and the US dollar was quoted at a small 25, and it had fallen to 18 taels and 5 qian. After 9:30, Hengxing, Yifeng, Yuda, Fuyu, Yuanheng, Dadecheng, Bingxing, etc. had very strong buying momentum, and HSBC bought British gold at 10 pence 5625 and also bought US dollars at 35 yuan 625, so the gold price rose by 5-6 taels.

The market was extremely sharp, reaching 25 taels. Later, there were ups and downs of 2 taels, and after 2:30, the Dalian Gang and Dadecheng continued to sell, falling back by 3 taels. At 3 o'clock, it was 17 taels and a half. Soon after, Yifeng, Tong Taixing, and others continued to advance without slackening, and rushed out of 20 taels again, with ups and downs of 2-3 taels in between. At 4 o'clock, it was 23 taels, and Fuchang, Bingxing, Maoyong, and retail investors sold, and then shaved off 4 taels, until the market closed at 4:30 at 18 taels and 8 qian, and then suppressed to 18 taels or so, an increase of 22 taels compared to the previous day (according to the listed price). The maximum for the whole day was 25 taels, and the minimum was 09 taels, a difference of 16 taels. The physical goods were 09 taels in the morning market, 20 taels at noon, 16 taels in the afternoon, and 18 taels at the close of the market. The listed price was 688 taels, with a deduction of about 70 taels, and the book price was 22 taels. The pre-market replenishment water was 22 taels, the post-market was 19 taels, and the red strip was added to 9 taels 25.

▲Guang Gang Covers Shorts, Dalian Sells More Trading on the Table, each goes its own way. According to statistics, Hengxing, Shengda, Yuancheng Yong, Fuyu, Hengchang Yong, Taifengcheng, Yuda, Yifeng Yong, Yifeng, Qianchangxiang, and Bingxing all advanced, while Yuantai, Tong Taichang, Yuanheng, Yuanxingyong, and Daxingyong had quite a lot of incoming and outgoing. Securities and Bonds Resume Downward Trend

Yesterday, at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, in the bond market, only a few varieties such as the Unified Tax 1934 were offered for spot trading. Trading volume remained sparse. Major investors adopted a wait-and-see attitude. Although sellers did not offer large amounts for sale, the selling pressure was still stronger than the buying, leading to a general decline in bond prices. In the morning sessions, prices of all bonds fell, but the momentum was sluggish, with only slight fluctuations, dropping only about 3 or 4 jiao compared to the previous day. Observing the trend of the bond market, it remains as sluggish as before. Its future fate will continue to depend on the development of the diplomatic situation. Cotton Yarn Market: Downturn Resurges

The yarn market is very weak, and the downward trend is intensifying. Due to the many national crises and widespread rumors, combined with extremely tight credit, public sentiment has become uneasy. Furthermore, some manufacturers are hedging their purchases, weakening the market further. Speculators are inclined to sell, making the situation even worse. Actual sales in the market are affected by financial conditions, and demand is lacking due to the turmoil of the times.

In the morning opening of the foreign cotton yarn futures market, due to the downward trend of American cotton, market sentiment was very loose. Joint Meeting of the Military, Police, and Local Defense Corps Yesterday - Measures to Maintain Public Order

▲Joint Military-Police-Corps Office to Be Established in Zhabei▲Mayor Zhang Expresses Responsibility for Protecting Public Order

The Japanese have been plotting and scheming in various commercial ports in China, such as Tianjin, Shanghai, and Wuhan, using despicable means to create disturbances and destruction, in order to deceive various countries and achieve their cunning plan of not withdrawing troops. Since receiving the alert about the Tianjin Incident, the military and police in this city have received intelligence from various sources that more than 200 Japanese ruffians have colluded with local criminals in this city, hoping to instigate a major riot to disrupt public order in this city. Therefore, in order to prevent such incidents from occurring, the authorities of the Shanghai Municipal Government Garrison Headquarters sent competent officials to conduct strict investigations. At the same time, a joint meeting of the military, police, and local defense corps was held at the municipal government at 2 p.m. yesterday.

Representatives from the Garrison Headquarters, the Public Security Bureau Water Patrol Team, and the Local Defense Corps attended the meeting. Mayor Zhang Qun also personally attended the meeting. The discussion lasted a long time, and it was not until after 5 p.m. that the meeting ended. After the meeting, according to Mayor Zhang's report, the results of the discussion can be summarized as follows: The city's public order prevention measures are very thorough, and there are specific plans. Although Japanese ruffians have repeatedly provoked trouble, they have been stopped immediately. However, it is said that there are Japanese ruffians colluding with criminals to instigate a riot, so in order to prevent such incidents from occurring, a more detailed plan was discussed at today's joint meeting of the military, police, and local defense corps. The discussion resulted in a very detailed plan. In order to facilitate the exchange of information, mutual communication, and effective prevention among the three parties - the military, police, and local defense corps - it was decided to establish a joint military-police-corps office of Shanghai Municipality in Zhabei, so as to make prevention of public order and protection of citizens more convenient and thorough.

Mayor Zhang also stated responsibly that he is always responsible for maintaining public order and citizen safety in the city. In addition to striving for thoroughness in prevention, he also dares to declare to the citizens that public order in the city can be peaceful and safe and that no accidents will occur.

Increased Patrols in the Chinese Areas Today

▲The Municipal Public Security Bureau

Today is the Prime Minister's birthday, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau is deeply concerned that general troublemakers may take advantage of the opportunity to create disturbances and disrupt public order. It has ordered the district chiefs of each district to strictly order their subordinate police officers to strengthen prevention. The police stations in charge of the areas bordering the Chinese Concession have been fully armed to prevent disturbances and maintain the usual state of martial law.

▲The Public Concession

The public security authorities in the Public Concession believe that there may be reactionary elements inciting ignorant people to take advantage of the Prime Minister's birthday to create riots, so the General Inspector's Office has issued a notice to all police stations to strengthen prevention. Police stations in Hongkou, Huishan, Gordon Road, Yangshupu, and other areas are particularly vigilant because they are located on the border or are areas where Japanese laborers congregate. Chinese and Western detectives and police officers will all be out on patrol today to avoid accidents.

▲The French Concession

All police stations in the French Concession received orders from their superiors yesterday stating that today is the Prime Minister's birthday and that they should pay attention to protection. Therefore, today, police stations on Avenue Edward VII, Avenue des Deux Rois, Rue Montauban, and other roads have sent Chinese and Western detectives and plainclothes police officers to patrol secretly. Other armed police officers are also patrolling in their respective jurisdictions to prevent accidents.

Shanghai Municipal Executive Committee's Proclamation to the Public Regarding the Fourth National Congress

▲ Listing Five Points… Announcing to All Sectors

The Fourth National Congress of the Chinese Kuomintang commenced its opening ceremony in Nanjing today. The representatives selected from this city, with the exception of Wu Kaixian who had already proceeded to Nanjing the day before yesterday, including Pan Gongzhan, Zhu Yingpeng, Wang Yansong, Hou Dachun, Zhang Tinghao, Chen Xizeng, etc., also departed last night to attend. The Shanghai Special Municipality Party Executive Committee, for the opening of the Fourth National Congress yesterday, specially issued a proclamation to the public, listing the five major significances of this congress. The original text is recorded as follows: Beloved citizens, today is the birthday of the Premier, and at the same time, our party is holding the Fourth National Congress in the capital. The convocation of this Fourth National Congress is indeed of the utmost significance. First, to safeguard the historical foundation of the party, our party, since its establishment, has transitioned from the Revive China Society, the Tongmenghui, the Chinese Revolutionary Party, to the Chinese Kuomintang. Although the names have been changed repeatedly, and the organization has been altered many times, the revolutionary doctrine and the revolutionary cause have remained completely consistent. Since the reorganization of our party in the thirteenth year of the Republic, there have been a total of three National Congresses. The first was held in Guangzhou in January of the thirteenth year, the second was held in Guangzhou in January of the fifteenth year, and the third was delayed until March of the eighteenth year due to the Northern Expedition and the purification of the party, before it could be held in Nanjing. The convocation of this Fourth National Congress is to continue the lineage of the Third National Congress, to safeguard the historical foundation of our party, so that our party can be further promoted and fulfill its historical mission. Therefore, safeguarding the foundation and building on the past is the most important significance of convening this congress. Second, to promote the effectiveness of party governance, our party, according to the mission given by the revolution and in accordance with the Premier's revolutionary strategy, represents the people in exercising political power during the military administration and tutelage periods, and undertakes the work of nation-building and governing the country. The mission is truly of utmost importance. Since the beginning of national unification and the implementation of tutelage, considerable achievements have been made in nation-building, and party governance has gradually gotten on track. In the future, we should continue to build on this grand plan, intensify the promotion of the effectiveness of party governance, and strive to achieve rapid progress in construction and complete the tutelage work as scheduled. The National Congress, as the highest authority of our party, has the full responsibility to promote the effectiveness of party governance. Therefore, the convocation of this National Congress is a major initiative to promote the effectiveness of party governance. Third, to strengthen the party's organization and unity, if our party is to complete the mission of nation-building and governing the country as scheduled, we must first seek to strengthen the party itself and unite the comrades within the party. Otherwise, if the party itself is not yet sound, how can it govern the country? If the comrades within the party cannot unite, how can they seek to strengthen the party? Therefore, knowing whether the historical mission of our party can be completed quickly depends entirely on whether the party itself can be sound and whether the comrades within the party can unite. In the past, the organization of our party was relatively sound, and comrades were generally able to unite sincerely, which enabled us to overcome reaction and govern the country. In the future, the party should continue to intensify the unity among comrades, in order to further strengthen the party itself. The convocation of this National Congress is an important gathering to intensify the practical unity of comrades within the party and to strengthen the organization of the party itself. Fourth, to consolidate the unity and peace of the party and the country, the greatest suffering felt by the whole country in recent years has been war and poverty. Therefore, we yearn for peace and unity to eliminate war, and for economic development to alleviate suffering. Comrades of our party and the people of the whole country have sacrificed countless lives and properties to create the unified and peaceful situation of today. This hard-won and most valuable achievement should be protected by the will and strength of all party members and the people of the whole country, and further efforts should be made in economic development to alleviate the suffering after natural disasters and wars. The convocation of this National Congress is a major measure to respond to the aspirations and needs of the people of the whole country, concentrate the will and strength of the entire party, to consolidate the peace and unity of the party and the country, and to alleviate the suffering of the people. Fifth, to concentrate the strength of the entire party to face the national crisis together, the purpose of our party's revolution is to eliminate feudal warlords and overthrow imperialism. For several years, we have aimed at this goal, fighting against warlords and imperialism. Now, domestic warlords have been initially eliminated through the efforts of comrades of our party and the assistance of the people. However, the Japanese imperialists, taking advantage of our national disasters and misfortunes, disregarding all national laws and justice, have blatantly invaded Liaoning and Jilin, plundering our property, burning our cities, raping our women, and killing our officials. This barbaric atrocity is unprecedentedly tragic. Our party, faced with this national humiliation, vows to concentrate the strength of the entire party to fight a decisive battle with the brutal Japanese, so as to ensure that the complete Chinese territory and sovereignty are not damaged, and to achieve the goal of overthrowing Japanese imperialism. Our party's convocation of this National Congress has the most important mission of facing the national crisis together and washing away the national humiliation. Chinese Kuomintang Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee.

Minutes of the Standing Committee Meeting of the Anti-Japanese Association

▲ The Seventeenth Meeting

The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association held its seventeenth Standing Committee meeting yesterday in the conference room of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Committee members present included Wang Xiaolai, Lu Jingshi, Yu Qiaqing, Fu Dewei, Fang Jiaobo, Lin Kanghou, etc. Fang Jiaobo was publicly elected as chairman, and Zhao Shusheng and Tong Yikang served as recorders. Decisions were made on the following cases: (1) Discussion of a letter from the Chinese Cotton Mill Federation regarding the request to release Japanese Toyota automatic looms purchased by the association's members, Dasheng and Zhenxin Companies, on July 28 of this year, which were registered with the Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Association and recently shipped to Shanghai by Nippon Yusen. (2) Discussion of a proposal by Committee Member Yu Zhongxian of the Twelfth Executive Committee that the association should specify a date for returning the account books that were reviewed to investigate goods entering various stores, in order to alleviate the difficulties of businesses. The general principle was approved by the general meeting, and the date was handed over to the association for determination. Please make a public decision on this case. Decision: (A) After copying the relevant accounts, the account books will be returned with a seal and signature of both parties covering the seam. (B) If the situation is complicated and cannot be returned immediately, it must not exceed seven days at the latest, but each department must not delay for more than two days. The method will remain the same as before. (3) Discussion of a report from the Investigation Department that Guangyuan Sugar Company privately sold more than 1,500 bags of Japanese sugar in July, August, and September, which has been verified. Please take appropriate action. Decision: Investigate this case quickly along with other cases. (4) Discussion of a letter from Liu Hongsheng regarding the proposal to continue purchasing white poplar branches from Huachang. Please follow the previous practice and consult the Inspection Department to notify each inspection office to release them. What should be done? Decision: Follow the practice. (5) A letter from the Japanese Students Anti-Japanese Association regarding the illegal detention of the association's executive committee members and the confiscation of all documents and seals by the French Concession police. Please provide assistance. What should be done? Decision: Handed over to the Investigation Department. (6) Discussion of a letter from American Hyatt regarding the association's illegal detention of bran and the request for compensation for losses. What should be done? Decision: Disapproved. (7) Discussion of the proposal to formulate detailed methods for issuing certificates of origin for goods, which has been reviewed by Committee Member Fang Jiaobo. Please approve and implement it to benefit commerce. Decision: Three committee members, Lin Kanghou, Xi Yushu, will review this. (8) The association has been established for several months. Please appoint members to start editing a work report. Decision: The secretariat will set a deadline of one month for each department to prepare their reports, which will be submitted to the secretariat and handled in conjunction with the Propaganda Department. (9) Discussion of a letter from the Knitting Industry Trade Association requesting that the illegally sealed yarn be unsealed immediately so that it can be used within the prescribed limit. What should be done? Decision: Discuss this again after reviewing the reports from each department. (10) Discussion of a letter from Xu Yongzuo, CPA, stating that the accounting affairs of the association's accounting section have been clearly taken over and that the handover list is being sent to the association for filing. Please review the case. (Attached: one copy of the handover list) Decision: The previous accounts will be sent to the CPA association for review, and a report will be made to the general meeting. (11) Discussion of a letter from Yu Binqi regarding a Chinese typewriter invented by him. However, the anti-Japanese news reported by the association stated that the typewriter was a Japanese product masquerading as a domestic product. He is sending a bayonet and is willing to die by this bayonet if it is indeed a Japanese product masquerading as a domestic product. Please investigate and clarify the matter and make a statement to all sectors. What should be done? (Attached: one bayonet) Decision: Handed over to the Investigation Department for review and reply within three days. (Three letters to all sectors and businesses are recorded separately below.)

▲ Announcement to All Sectors on the Commencement of Collecting National Salvation Funds

Public Announcement No. 14 of the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association states: Based on the resolution of the Shanghai All Sectors Representatives Conference, the method and reporting form for collecting national salvation funds have been determined and sent to various Chinese banks, money shops, and trust companies in the city for collection. Each collecting institution will stamp its official seal, or have it signed and stamped by the deputy manager, and issue receipts as proof. Refusal to accept is not allowed. A report must be submitted to the association every ten days. Now that the national crisis is becoming more urgent and funds are in great need, the collection of this national salvation fund will commence immediately. We urge all compatriots to contribute generously and sacrifice their families to relieve the national crisis. The use of the national salvation fund must be decided by the general meeting and announced in the newspaper before it can be used. Each collecting institution will not bear any responsibility. This announcement is hereby made.

▲ Letter to Various Businesses Regarding the Addition of a "Non-Japanese Goods" Mark

The Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association yesterday sent a notice to various institutions, organizations, companies, and businesses: We are writing to inform you that the Shanghai CPA Association Standing Committee Xi Yushu and others have suggested to our association that the personnel of all institutions, organizations, companies, and businesses should be advised by the responsible personnel to not purchase Japanese goods. If there is a violation, the person should be immediately dismissed, and the responsible person will bear the responsibility and be permanently banned. All businesses selling goods must add a mark on the invoice stating "This product is definitely not a Japanese product. If it is not true, a penalty of ten times the price will be imposed." so that purchasers who cannot identify the goods will not mistakenly purchase them. We hope that you will consider these suggestions separately and implement them in practice. It is essential to have a determination to resist Japan, and boycotting goods must be sustained. The methods proposed by Mr. Xi and others enable people to take responsibility for themselves and monitor each other, which is indeed appropriate and effective. We hope that all institutions, organizations, companies, and businesses will fulfill their duties and follow suit. With clear responsibilities, the center will be honest. We also hope that our patriotic compatriots will refuse to purchase goods that cannot be identified unless the store adds a responsible mark. We hereby notify you, hoping for your attention and consideration.

▲ Store Managers Are Not Allowed to Suppress National Salvation Movements

The Anti-Japanese Association yesterday also notified store managers that they should not suppress apprentices from engaging in national salvation movements: We are writing to inform you that since the outbreak of the Japanese disaster, the whole country has been in an uproar. Our compatriots from all sectors have been aroused by righteous indignation, running around weeping and engaging in national salvation movements. However, our association has repeatedly received letters from workers and apprentices in the commercial and industrial sectors stating that they have been subjected to oppression by store owners or managers due to differences in positions. They are often angry and ashamed when they discourage the entry of Japanese goods, resulting in being suspended from their jobs or being abused. This situation is extremely hateful. Therefore, we specially announce to store managers from all sectors that if there are any more cases of suppressing workers and apprentices from engaging in national salvation movements, the oppressed person is allowed to report it to the association for punishment. Please take note of this matter.

The Great Alliance for Promoting National Products Held a Representatives' Meeting Yesterday

▲ Discussing the issue of rescuing raw materials for national product factories ▲ Scheduling a reception for leaders from all sectors to express their opinions

The Committee of the Great Alliance for Promoting National Products held a factory representatives' meeting of the four national product groups at 2:00 PM yesterday at Nine Acers to discuss important issues. The atmosphere of the entire venue was very tense, and several important cases were resolved. The details of each situation are recorded separately below.

▲ Attending Groups The four groups, including the China National Products Maintenance Association, the Shanghai Citizens' Association for Promoting National Products, the Shanghai Machine-Made National Products Factories Federation, and the Shanghai National Products Factories Federation, and their affiliated factory members, Sanyou Industrial Society, Anlu Cotton Weaving Factory, Great China Celluloid Factory, Zhenhua Paint Factory, Tianchu MSG Factory, Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory, Zhonghua Industrial Factory, Huachang Manufacturing Factory, Guanshengyuan, Yixin Toothbrush Factory, Zhonghua Iron Factory, Hongxing Socks Factory, Zhonghua Enamel Factory, etc., a total of more than 300 factory representatives including Ji Jiannan, Wang Jiean, Wang Hanqiang, and Chen Yiting, etc., more than 400 people.

(4) The table of Japanese raw materials will be distributed to each factory today for completion. (5) The national product tea party will be handed over to the preparatory committee for further action. (6) All factories unanimously support the Great Alliance for Promoting National Products. (7) The restoration of the national product market will be discussed at the next meeting. The meeting adjourned at 8:00 PM.

Regular Inspection of Weights and Measures in Four Districts Including Zhabei

▲ The Social Affairs and Public Safety Bureaus Formulate Inspection Procedures ▲ Inspections Scheduled to Commence on the 18th of This Month

Following the unification of weights and measures in this city on July 1st of this year, the Social Affairs and Public Safety Bureaus jointly formulated a schedule for the regular inspection of the Hu Nan district. The Weights and Measures Verification Institute, in conjunction with the various district offices, dispatched personnel daily to conduct inspections, which have now been completed. It is now learned that the aforementioned bureaus have also formulated a schedule for the regular inspection of the four districts of Zhabei, Pudong, Wusong, and Jiangwan, which has been jointly announced and is scheduled to commence on the 18th of this month. Anyone found using old measures at that time will be punished according to the law. The announcement and inspection schedule are appended below. The matter concerns the joint announcement that, regarding the unification of weights and measures in this city with a deadline of July 1st of this year, an order was presented to and approved by the Ministry of Industry and subsequently relayed by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations to their respective members, instructing them to uniformly adopt the new system. Furthermore, a schedule for the regular inspection of the Hu Nan district was formulated, and the Weights and Measures Verification Institute, together with the various district offices, dispatched personnel daily to conduct separate inspections, which have been completed and recorded. Now, in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the Regulations for the Implementation of Inspection of Weights and Measures in this city, a schedule for the regular inspection of the four districts of Zhabei, Pudong, Wusong, and Jiangwan has been formulated. We hereby issue this joint announcement to inform all merchants and residents that it will be implemented from November 18th, commencing the regular inspection of the four districts. Anyone found using old measures will be punished immediately according to the law, without any leniency. Everyone must strictly comply and not violate this order. This is the announcement. Attached is the second phase schedule of regular inspection of weights and measures, categorized by industry and district: Zhabei District, Pudong District, Jiangwan District, Wusong District.

Health Bureau to Regularly Vaccinate Factory Workers Against Smallpox

▲ From the 16th to the End of December

The Municipal Health Bureau considers smallpox to be a legally defined infectious disease, which is extremely harmful once contracted. To prevent epidemics, it dispatches personnel twice a year, in spring and autumn, in accordance with Article 6 of the Ministry's promulgated Vaccination Regulations, to factories of all sizes throughout the city to vaccinate all staff and workers' children against smallpox for prevention. It is reported that the period for factory vaccination has been set from the 16th of this month to the end of December. All factories were notified yesterday so that personnel can be sent to administer vaccinations at the appropriate time.

Suspension of North and South Ocean Shipping Routes by Japanese Steamships

▲ Citing Tianjin Unrest as Pretext ▲ Dismissing Chinese Employees

▲ Japanese merchant ships suspend sailings on the Tianjin-Shanghai-Tianjin route. Kawasaki Kisen Kaisha operates two ships, the Keisaki Maru and the Heiryū Maru, transporting Japanese goods to North China, and their business is quite good. Recently, since the Japanese disturbed Tianjin, Japanese warships were dispatched to Tianjin. Japanese merchant ships in Tianjin are under the protection of the navy. Yesterday, Kawasaki Kisen Kaisha decided to abolish the Tianjin route. The Keisaki Maru is scheduled to suspend operations from tomorrow, and the Heiryū Maru will cease operations on the 15th. After these ships stop serving the North Ocean route, they will be redeployed to Taiwan.

▲ Nisshin Shosen Kaisha reduces the number of coastal routes. Nisshin Shosen Kaisha's Yangtze River ships have already been suspended. Currently, the company still operates two coastal routes: one is the North Ocean route, served by the Kwasan Maru and the Tozan Maru; the other is the South China route, served by the Rosan Maru and the Suzan Maru. In the past two months, North and South Ocean ports have unanimously boycotted Japan. The company's four ships often sail empty. Recently, stevedores and barge workers in Shantou, Amoy, and other ports have also resisted. With the unrest in Tianjin, the company decided yesterday that the excessive losses from sailing empty ships are too great, but suspending operations would risk losing the routes. A compromise was proposed: one ship on each of the North and South Ocean routes will be temporarily suspended, leaving the Rosan Maru and the Kwasan Maru to maintain the routes with difficulty. This can be implemented next week.

▲ Japanese ships dismiss Chinese staff. More than ten Japanese ships have been suspended, resulting in a considerable number of Chinese sailors and other crew members losing their jobs. Nisshin Shosen Kaisha alone has more than 3,500 Chinese sailors, crew members, and office staff in various ports. Since this month, about 2,000 have been dismissed due to ship suspensions. Another 160-170 are expected to be dismissed next week.

Ship Collision in Fog on the Huangpu River

▲ Japanese Ship Collides with Japanese Warship. Due to fog in this city the last two days, ships entering and leaving the port have been delayed. The Japanese cruiser Tokiwa Maru, anchored in the Huangpu River at the tenth buoy, was struck by the Japanese ship Saiho Maru at 8:20 a.m. yesterday. As two barges were passing by, the Saiho Maru was unable to avoid them and struck the warship's outer shell of the first compartment. The warship, anchored in the river, was unable to move aside, resulting in damage to the outer hull of the bow compartment by the Saiho Maru, measuring approximately 15 feet in length. Repairs are underway.

The Japanese ship Paris Damaged. The Osaka Company's Paris Maru, arriving in Shanghai from Europe, was anchored in the Huangpu River at the fifteenth buoy, unloading cargo. At 8:15 a.m. on the 9th, the fog had not yet dissipated, and the river was completely obscured. A small steamship passing by the outer side suddenly encountered another ship. The small steamship avoided as usual, but its bow struck the left side of the Paris Maru, damaging the steel plates. The small steamship also sustained minor damage. Yesterday, the Osaka Company sent personnel to inspect the damage, and repairs will be carried out in Shanghai.

Zheng Gongyao, Captain of the Minsheng Warship, Takes Office Today

▲ Total Crew of 98 Officers and Men ▲ Sails to the Capital for Military Exercises After the Flag Raising

The Minsheng warship, the fifth new vessel built by the Naval Ministry, will raise its flag today, and the ship's captain will be sworn into office. Details are as follows:

▲ Captain Takes Office. Zheng Gongyao, the captain of the ship, is a staff colonel and commander of the Naval Training Fleet. Having received the order to assume his new post, he reported for duty on the first of this month. The vice-captain, Nie Xiyu, is transferred from the vice-captain position on the Minquan warship. Both will be sworn into office simultaneously at 9:00 a.m. today on the ship. In addition to inviting various ship captains to participate, Chen Jiliang, the commander of the First Naval Fleet, will represent the Naval Ministry to administer the oath.

▲ Total Officers and Crew. The ship's total officers and crew, excluding service personnel, number 98. Currently appointed by the Ministry, in addition to the two captains Zheng and Nie, there are also Chief Engineer Huang Yiqing, Gunnery Officer Xu Renhao, Chief Electrical Officer He Sijing, Navigation Officer Lang Jiancheng, Assistant Engineers Xu Zhenqian and Lin Jia, and Secretary Guo Shaochang (the medical officer has not yet been appointed by the Ministry). The remaining 86 are soldiers.

▲ Sails to the Capital Today. The ship received an order from the Naval Ministry yesterday, instructing it to sail to Baguazhou in the capital today after the ship's captain is sworn into office and the flag is officially raised, to participate in military exercises for inspection. Therefore, the ship was fired up yesterday, ready to depart. It is scheduled to make its maiden voyage to the capital around 10:00 a.m. today after the flag raising.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Exemption from Disinfection Fees for Inland Harbor Vessels

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the National Seaport Quarantine Bureau yesterday, requesting free disinfection for vessels in the inner harbor. The letter stated: "We are writing to you regarding the letter received on the 11th of this month from the Inland River Steamer Industry Association, concerning the National Seaport Quarantine Bureau's enforcement of fees. The association states that there is no precedent for such fees, and inland river vessels travel very short distances and are free from epidemics, making disinfection unnecessary. On October 21st, the association wrote to your esteemed organization, requesting that you present this matter to the Social Affairs Bureau and request that it be stopped, and also requested the Public Security Bureau to delay sending police to assist the bureau in collecting fees. Subsequently, we received your letter No. Pu Zi 1194, stating that it had been submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for consultation on cancellation and that the Public Security Bureau had been asked to mediate. A reply would be sent separately after receiving the response. Later, we received your letter No. Pu Zi 1290, stating that the Public Security Bureau replied that the National Seaport Quarantine Bureau is under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Interior and should be asked to explain the matter. Since this matter has been submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for consultation on revocation, it should be handled by the bureau, and there is no need to submit it directly to the Ministry of Interior. We await the Social Affairs Bureau's decision. However, the Quarantine Bureau continues to send Chinese and foreign personnel to forcibly collect fees from various shipping companies, and their actions are even more aggressive than before. Yesterday, the Association's member, Xie Xing Shipping Company, reported that the Quarantine Bureau had been forcing them to pay fees for days. When they explained that they were in the process of consulting on cancellation, the Quarantine Bureau replied, 'We only know about collecting fees, nothing else,' and threatened to pry off the ship's plate and detain the ship. They also forced the company's employees to go to the Quarantine Bureau to make a statement and said that they would come back tomorrow to collect the fees, and if they still did not pay, they would not be lenient. Merchants are timid and fear government officials like gods. Even if they have a reason, how would they dare to argue with them? Moreover, with the collaboration of the water patrol officers, they can implement the threat to detain the ship with a single word, which would inevitably lead to the stagnation of the shipping industry. Therefore, we are writing to you again, requesting that your esteemed organization write to the Social Affairs Bureau to stop this and immediately write to the Second Squadron of the Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team (Captain Li, address at Xin Zha Bridge) to delay sending personnel to assist the Quarantine Bureau in collecting fees, so that we can quietly await the Social Affairs Bureau's decision. We have learned that our association sent a letter to your esteemed organization on August 12th, stating that the fee schedule attached to the Quarantine Regulations does not explicitly mention fees for small boats and requested an explanation. Your esteemed organization did not respond. It was not until October 24th that you sent the Regulations for Disinfection of Inland Harbor Vessels to the respective associations, which included the text of separate fees. However, your esteemed organization began collecting fees from small boats around July 20th of this year. The time of fee collection was more than three months apart from the time of formulating the regulations. It is not known on what basis the fees were collected before. Moreover, the disinfection of inland harbor vessels is a novel initiative. Your esteemed organization's letter of October 24th also mentioned that misunderstandings often occur. Therefore, public sentiment must be respected, and the attitude in dealing with matters should be peaceful. When the city launched the business tax, it widely solicited opinions from merchants and residents, held meetings for discussion, and deliberated repeatedly. It has been almost a year, and implementation is still pending, which demonstrates the fair and peaceful attitude of the municipal authorities. The fees collected by your esteemed organization from small boats are essentially a type of handling fee, which should not be equated with municipal taxes. However, you did not invite the relevant industries to openly discuss the matter beforehand. Instead, you detained ships and plates with utmost severity. In your esteemed organization's letter of October 24th, those who raised even the slightest doubt were even treated as stubborn and ignorant. Compared with the city authorities' handling of the business tax, merchants and residents are truly disappointed with the way your esteemed organization has handled things. Our association holds a fair and impartial view that your esteemed organization's expenses are allocated monthly by the Customs Office and do not rely on inner harbor disinfection fees for funding. All disinfection of inner harbor vessels should be provided free of charge so that public sentiment is not aroused. In addition to having telegraphed the Ministry of Interior separately, we are writing this letter to consult you, hoping that you will investigate and handle the matter and provide a response. This is addressed to the National Seaport Quarantine Bureau."

Second Kidnapping of the President of the Siming Bank

▲ Chen Yanghe is Already Sixty Years Old ▲ Abducted Yesterday While Driving Home from Qilu

▲ Suddenly Abducted by Bandits En Route ▲ The Chauffeur Was Helpless

Chen Yanghe, the current vice president of the Siming Bank and a native of Ningbo, was suddenly kidnapped by bandits last night. The details are as follows:

▲ Respected in the Banking Industry. Chen is 60 years old this year and lives at No. 17 Siming Village (formerly Chenghe Village) on Foch Road in the French Concession. He has worked at the Siming Bank for many years and is a respected figure in the banking industry. Every day after work, around 7:00 or 8:00 p.m., Chen would go to the Qilu Club on Songshan Road in the French Concession to play mahjong for entertainment. This was his daily routine, and he always used his blue car for transportation, with Concession license plate No. 7762 and Municipal plate No. 207, rain or shine. This attracted the attention of bandits.

▲ Four Bandits Jumped Out. Last night, Chen went as usual. Around 9:00 p.m., the mahjong game ended, and he prepared to return home. The chauffeur, Zhong Atao, started the car, intending to drive straight home. Unexpectedly, as they approached the entrance of No. 865 Foch Road, a car suddenly drove towards them from the east. The car was moving very slowly, directly facing Chen's car. The chauffeur, Zhong Atao, quickly braked the car and was about to argue with the oncoming car when four bandits suddenly jumped out of the car, each holding a pistol and warning them to remain silent.

▲ Forcibly Pulled Chen into the Bandits' Car. The four bandits rushed towards Chen's car, first smashing a piece of the right-side window and brandishing their guns to warn them to keep silent. Then, they opened the car door, dragged Chen out of the car, and forced him into the bandits' car, which sped away at full speed and disappeared in an instant. The chauffeur, Atao, witnessed his master being kidnapped and shouted for help. By the time the nearby detectives arrived, it was too late. He then drove the car to the French police station to report the incident. Upon hearing the report, the police chief immediately dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to search in all directions, but to no avail.

▲ Once Kidnapped Last Year. Afterwards, the police station notified Chen's family by telephone and questioned the chauffeur in detail, asking if he had clearly seen the license plate of the bandits' car. He claimed that he was in a state of panic at the time his master was abducted, and when he looked back, the taillights of the car were completely dark, and the speed was very fast, making it impossible to discern the details. He only saw that the bandits' car was a black covered car. He also said that Chen had been kidnapped once in August last year on Chengdu Road but was soon ransomed. This was the second time he had been abducted.

Various Charity Groups Discuss Continuing to Operate the Refugee Shelter

▲ Extending for Another Four Months ▲ Expenses Separately Determined

Yesterday at 5:00 p.m., the National Flood Relief Committee, the Shanghai Charity Federation, the Chinese and Foreign Relief Committee, the Chinese Red Cross Society, the Various Provinces Flood Disaster Relief Associations, and the Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association, six charitable organizations, held a temporary joint meeting at Renji Hall on 6th Ma Road to discuss the Shanghai refugee shelter. Attendees included Wang Yiting, Huang Hanzhi, Xu Junren, Ye Kaixin, Lu Bohong, Wang Binyan, Chen Liangyu, Lu Shao-Liu, Cheng Yiqing (representing Lu), Zhu Ziqiao, Qu Wenliu, and Cha Liangzhao. Xu Junren chaired the meeting, and Xiao Zhantong recorded the proceedings. First, Mr. Lu Bohong reported on the current pitiful condition of the flood refugees in the shelter, stating that there were approximately 6,000 refugees, requiring 30,000 yuan per month, or at least 120,000 yuan for four months. The Social Affairs Bureau would operate the shelter until the 15th, and it was proposed to continue operating it for another four months. The six charitable organizations were requested to jointly raise 120,000 yuan. The National Flood Relief Committee agreed to raise 25,000 yuan, the Chinese and Foreign Relief Committee agreed to raise 20,000 yuan, the Red Cross Society agreed to raise 20,000 yuan, the Shanghai Charity Federation agreed to raise 10,000 yuan, the Various Provinces Flood Disaster Relief Associations agreed to raise 25,000 yuan, and the Jiangsu Flood Disaster Relief Association agreed to raise 20,000 yuan, for a total of 120,000 yuan. Lu Bohong, Zhu Shoucheng, Wang Binyan, and Chen Liangyu were elected to handle the reception and subsequent shelter matters, and various measures were discussed: (1) Name: renamed the Shanghai Municipal Refugee Shelter Committee; (2) Elect representatives to contact the Municipal Government: Wang Yiting, Qu Wenliu, Huang Hanzhi, Lu Bohong, and Wang Binyan were elected to contact the Municipal Government on the 13th; (3) Elect drafters of the articles of association: Xu Junren, Qu Wenliu, and Huang Hanzhi were elected; (4) Formulate shelter measures and quotas: it was agreed that efforts should be made to persuade and repatriate refugees while providing shelter, and the maximum number of refugees should be limited to the existing housing; (5) Shelter arrangements: it was agreed that this would be decided during the drafting of the articles of association. It was also agreed that the Bihan Shelter should be managed by the Refugee Shelter Committee as the Nanshi Shelter. The meeting adjourned as the clock struck seven.

▲ Case Cracked by the Fifth District Police Station

Xu Kesheng, a local resident living at No. 11 Hengye Lane, Hengye Road, Tongji Road, Zhabei, is one of the shareholders of the local real estate company. His family is quite wealthy, so he has become the target of bandits. Since the 13th of the month, he has been receiving extortion letters, totaling nine, demanding a large sum of money and arranging a meeting near the bamboo fence in an empty field near Wangjia Wooden Bridge. Xu initially dismissed this type of anonymous extortion as commonplace in Shanghai and paid no attention to it. However, the wording of the last few letters was quite aggressive, and Xu's elderly mother was very worried. Xu could no longer tolerate it and took the previous letters to the Fifth District Police Station to report the matter. Chief Wang immediately ordered Inspector Wang Zhizhang to handle the matter properly. Inspector Wang waited at the designated address several times, but there was no sign of the bandits. Until the 6th of this month, the bandits sent another letter, arranging for Xu to write a reply last night and leave it on the bamboo fence at Wangjia Wooden Bridge. Inspector Wang then instructed Xu to write a letter and supervised several police officers in disguising themselves as peddlers and ambushing the location. Around 10:00 p.m. that night, two people were seen wandering back and forth in the area several times. They reached out and took the reply letter from the bamboo fence. Inspector Wang bravely stepped forward and arrested the two men, taking them to the district for questioning. According to their confession, one was Xu A'gen, 30 years old, from Tongzhou, and the other was Xu Shengkou, 46 years old, also from Tongzhou. They confessed that the scheme was masterminded by their accomplices Xue Zhiming and Peng Xiaobing. Inspector Wang then arrested Xue at his address in Hong'an Lane, Mongol Road, as well as the suspects Pan A'jin, Xue Daoyuan, and Rong A'san, and others. At the same time, he also cooperated with the Public Concession Police to arrest Peng. Under questioning, Rong A'san confessed that he was 38 years old, Xue Daoyuan was 21 years old, and Pan A'jin was 26 years old. Their confessions were unusually cunning. After questioning, Chief Wang immediately sent all the suspects, along with the nine letters, to the Judicial Section for strict investigation.

Due to a conspiracy to seize the estate of the late Zhang Linsen in Huayuan Shiqiao, Zhang Qingxiang, the third son (also known as Zhang Fugeng), colluded with his maternal uncle Zhang Quansheng and his mother, Zhang Zhangshi, to plot the murder of his adopted son, Zhang Guoxiang. ▲Fan Quangen was interrogated again yesterday▲Re-trial scheduled due to incomplete witness testimony

Fan Quangen, who runs the Fan Zhenxing utensil shop in Zhenfuli, Chenjia浜 small vegetable market, Xinzha Bridge, paid for a ‘shulong’ (formal intimacy) in March with Lao Ba (original name Duan A’er), a servant in the house of prostitute Liu Yanyan at 321 Huile里, Fuzhou Road, agreeing on a price of 300 yuan, with 50 yuan paid upfront. However, after their one-time encounter, Duan did not come again. Upon being pursued for the debt, he ignored it. Duan A’er became depressed as a result. It was not until 2 p.m. the next day that the roommate discovered the body, but he had already died and rigor mortis had set in, making rescue impossible. Huang Li was then summoned, but because she had not arrived, she could not be questioned. The plaintiff also brought witness Xu Yuxiang, who stated that he accompanied Fan to Liu Yanyan’s place that day. There were guests in the main room, so he and Fan sat in a small room until 12 p.m. before leaving together. The judge asked if he and Fan had returned after 12 p.m. Xu replied that he went home at that time and did not know if Fan had gone back. As the witnesses were not yet complete, the court ordered a retrial next Wednesday. At this point, the plaintiff’s lawyer requested that the defendant be released on bail, while the defendant’s lawyer objected. After a lengthy debate between the two parties, Judge Feng ordered the defendant to be released on bail, subject to being available for questioning at any time, and then adjourned the court.

Transfer of Lake Bandit Wei Hongxiang

Wei Hongxiang (nicknamed Changban Ahe), a native of Shanyang and the leader of the lake bandits, used to be a captain under the command of Tai Bao Ashu, the already executed leader of the lake bandits. After Ashu was executed, Wei formed his own gang, leading hundreds of followers, specializing in robbery and kidnapping in the area bordering Songjiang and Jinshan, committing all kinds of evil deeds. The government had repeatedly sent detectives to track him down, but to no avail. Now, Fan Guozhong, the captain of the first patrol of the 洙泾 水警队 (Zhu Jing River Police), learned that the bandit leader was hiding in Shanghai. On the 7th of this month, he, along with Chinese and foreign detectives from the Public Concession Police, arrested the bandit Wei at the Shuangfengyuan teahouse at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Hector Road. He was taken to the police station and escorted to the First Special District Court for trial and extradition. Captain Fan has prepared a document and personally led his team to Shanghai to take the bandit Wei back to the First District Headquarters of the Minhang River Police and request that District Chief Xu bring him to justice.

Tenants of Yuxingfang Present a Document to the Municipal Government

The tenants of Yuxingfang, Laoshenfu Road, this city, yesterday presented a document to Mayor Zhang, stating, "Presenting a petition for speculation in real estate, causing hardship to the citizens, respectfully requesting that you quickly resolve this issue to benefit the residents." The houses in Yuxingfang, Laoshenfu Road, French Concession of Shanghai, have only been built for seven years. Initially, they were rented out by the British company, Taylor & Co. This spring, the management and rent collection were changed to Liu Chenglin, the director of the real estate department of the lawyer, Tibberk. Two months later, a notice of renovation was issued, asking the tenants to move out before August 1 of this year. The tenants replied according to law and requested that the Shanghai Real Estate Association mediate and continue to collect rent. However, on August 23 of this year, the tenants received a notice from lawyers Shen Qi and Wang Jianfan, representing Changli Company, asking them to vacate the premises by the end of August. At the same time, they also received a notice from the aforementioned real estate department, stating that the transfer of property rights should be announced and declared, otherwise the parties involved would inevitably be affected. Therefore, they sent a letter through the Shanghai Real Estate Association to Liu Chenglin, asking whether it was true, but no reply was received. Unexpectedly, around 3 p.m. on October 2 of this year, the French Water and Electricity Company sent craftsmen to cut off the water supply to the neighborhood, causing a major crisis in terms of life, hygiene, fire prevention, and safety for all residents. The tenants' representatives went to the Water and Electricity Company to inquire about the reason for the water cut. They were told that Liu Chenglin had not paid the water bills since August of this year, claiming that the property rights had been transferred. They went to the transferee mentioned by Liu Chenglin to collect the bills, but were told that the transfer had not been completed and they would not pay. The Water Company, unable to collect the water bills, had no choice but to cut off the water supply. The tenants then managed to raise money and paid off the water bills owed by the landlord. At 3 p.m. on October 5, the Water Company repaired the water source and continued to supply water. This matter has been reported to the Social Bureau for approval. The landlord, seeing that damaging the water source could not achieve the purpose of forced eviction, sent craftsmen to build bamboo fences on the 21st of this month at 9 a.m., hoping to imitate Huang Chu-jiu's actions towards Fuxingli on Zhejiang Road and the New Sassoon Bank's actions towards Qingyunli on Jiangxi Road, using force to demolish and evict the tenants. Now, the tenants continue to be threatened. According to the investigation, the houses were completed on June 1, 1924. At that time, the market was very sluggish. Those who moved in to live and do business expected that it would take at least twenty years for renovation to occur, according to Shanghai custom. Therefore, they paid huge sums of small rent and tips, and invested huge amounts of money in renovation, believing that they could recover the costs over twenty years. The two largest disputes over renting houses in Shanghai have been in litigation for years, all arising from the issue of the age of the houses. This kind of dispute is not initially a violation of the landlord's rights, but rather the exercise of rights that harms public order and good customs. After all, settling down in one's homeland is a virtue of the Chinese nation, and living and working in peace is the foundation of national wealth and strength. The landlord's arbitrary renovation of houses specifically for rent will destroy the national virtue of settling down in one's homeland and the psychology of living and working in peace, and will inevitably harm public order and good customs. According to the investigation, the price of the land and houses this spring was 156,000 Shanghai taels, which Liu Chenglin purchased and resold to the current landlord, becoming more than 200,000 taels. Liu Chenglin made a net profit of 35,000 taels in just six months, which shows the thickness of the speculative profits. Some say that speculation in real estate is no different from speculation in commodities and securities, but in fact, they cannot be compared. The profits and losses of speculation in commodities and securities are borne solely by the speculator. As for speculation in real estate, the profits are solely obtained by the speculator, and the losses are compensated by the tenants. For example, for securities with a face value of 100 yuan and an annual interest rate of 8%, if they are bought for 80 yuan, the annual interest rate is 1%. If the market interest rate is 1.6%, the speculator (i.e., the holder) cannot ask the issuer of the securities to increase the interest to fill their wishes, but can only sell them for cash and make another investment with an annual interest rate of 1.6%. The speculators in real estate are very different. For example, if they buy land and houses in area A, they initially do not care that the annual interest rate of the rent in that area is only 6%. They use the virtue of tenants settling down in their homeland, the psychology of living and working in peace, and the huge investment of small rent and renovation costs, or they first increase the rent unsuccessfully, followed by a notice of renovation, or they first issue a notice of renovation to achieve their purpose of increasing the rent, or they have already increased the rent and cannot immediately increase it again, so they pretend to transfer the property rights and change to another landlord, doing the same thing. As a result, after the rent is increased, the annual interest rate is 8%, and the selling price can be increased. For example, if it is bought for 100,000 taels of silver, it can be sold for more than 130,000 taels after this rent increase. In one transfer, a profit of more than 30,000 taels can be obtained, and this profit is the blood and sweat of the tenants. This is indeed an evil demon that creates serious social problems. Moreover, in recent years, real estate speculators have been concentrated in the Special Zone, which has a significant impact on the development of municipal administration outside the Special Zone. If this kind of real estate speculator is strictly sanctioned, social floating capital can be invested in other areas that urgently need development, and the method of sanction is to impose administrative restrictions on rent increases and renovations. Furthermore, this kind of real estate speculation fundamentally conflicts with your government's public housing plan, and is especially contrary to the principle of benefiting the residents in the National Construction Outline. After all, the construction of public housing by the public is often limited by public funds. If real estate speculation is sanctioned, the effect will be greater than the public construction of public housing. For the sake of the vast majority of citizens who rent houses in the city, for the sake of supporting the public construction of public housing, and for the sake of the principle of benefiting the residents in the National Construction Outline, we should submit a document for your review, humbly requesting that you stop the landlord's behavior of treating citizens as fish and meat, and relieve the citizens from their predicament. The city will be fortunate, and the citizens will be fortunate. Respectfully presented to Zhang, the mayor of the Shanghai Municipal Government.
