A Leading Catholic Orders Rejection of Drugs

▲The Catholic Church assists in rejecting drugs▲Archbishop Gang issues eight instructions

The China National Anti-Drug Association, in order to expand the power of the anti-drug military movement, had previously entrusted its member, former Premier Lu Zhengxiang, to request the Pope of the Roman Catholic Church to issue a general order to the national Catholic Church to carry out the anti-drug movement together. It was approved by the Pope, who commended the China National Anti-Drug Association and ordered that all Christian churches in the country should follow suit. It was heard that Dr. Wang Jingqi, the chairman of the association, went to Ping to work and was personally visited by Archbishop Gang, the representative of the Roman Curia in China, who expressed the church's willingness to cooperate sincerely with the Anti-Drug Association. In addition to issuing a general order to all churches in the country to follow suit, he also requested that the Anti-Drug Association send all the promotional materials for the anti-drug movement to the national Catholic Church. This was done, and Huang Jiawei, the director-general of the association, sent a letter of thanks to Archbishop Gang. The instructions of Archbishop Gang are translated as follows for compliance: In accordance with the regulations of the Shanghai Bishops' Conference regarding the prohibition of opium, it is necessary to order all bishops to abide by them. This chapter has fully stated the importance of the Catholic Church's relationship to the opium problem. Recently, the Secretary of State of the Holy See, Bassili, also sent a handwritten letter to Lu Zhengxiang, the former Minister of Foreign Affairs of China and the current monk in Loping (Belgium), stating that the Holy See's policy on the prohibition of opium remains unchanged. As the responsibility of this Archbishop lies, it is necessary to order all Catholic Churches in China to continue to assist in the anti-drug movement, so as to unify the steps and broaden the effectiveness. The following points are listed for compliance: (1) All pastors must be in awe of the Holy Teachings and must not overstep them. When administering the Holy Sacraments to the faithful, they should pay attention to whether the faithful and protectors have a smoking habit or are planting opium seedlings or selling opium and other similar behaviors when preserving the time of baptism. (2) Although planting and selling drugs are not illegal in China now, the result is tantamount to murder, which is greatly contrary to the Holy Law. (3) When preaching in churches, all pastors should take this opportunity to publicize to the faithful and protectors the harms of opium in terms of material and spiritual matters. (4) In all schools and publications, more efforts should be made to promote the purpose of rejecting drugs. The old and corrupt are deeply addicted and cannot be saved, but for the younger generation, we must make great wishes and urge them not to get addicted to smoking. If the government and public groups work together to carry out the movement, if the church can help, it will be quick and effective, and at least it will achieve good results in terms of future spiritual and material improvement. From the perspective of the relationship between the church and the country, as long as we have the determination and perseverance to cultivate young people, we can achieve results in the shortest possible time. (5) Rejecting drugs is a social propaganda policy, which is also in line with the purpose of preaching and uniting Catholic youth. All people in the church, whether old or young, should strive to help, so as to abide by the Holy Teachings and devote themselves to rejecting drugs. (6) Catholic Churches should issue various leaflets and pamphlets to help promote drug rejection. All such publications can be distributed to the faithful free of charge. (7) This Archbishop recently met with Dr. Wang Jingqi, the chairman of the China National Anti-Drug Association, and agreed to send various slogans, pictures, and other propaganda materials of the Anti-Drug Association to the eleven diocesan offices and Catholic schools of this Catholic Church. If a certain diocese needs a large number of propaganda materials, it can also contact the Anti-Drug Association directly. The Geneva International League's Commission on Narcotics has also entrusted this Catholic Church to devote itself to this social cause related to humanity. (8) The Chinese National Government should adopt a policy of prohibition (such as banning planting and transportation) in order to save this raging tide. This Catholic Church should also assist the Chinese government in educating and persuading it.

Page 16

national government to carry it out and strengthen its momentum. The method is to cooperate with the China National Anti-Drug Association. Our Lord Jesus will also sympathize with this move, because the good people in this large part of China, who are innocently suffering from this torture, cannot but arouse the compassion of Christ. A bishop who has been in China for a long time once said from experience that the world has also worked hard to fight against terrible diseases such as tuberculosis, liver cancer, and leprosy, but the above-mentioned diseases are not as harmful as opium, so why turn a blind eye to it? This is a prayer for the blessing of the teachings.

The District Branch Pleads for the Shantytown Dwellers of Haig Road

▲Request to forward to the Municipal Government▲Build public housing in West Shanghai as soon as possible

About 200 households of poor people living in thatched sheds along the eastern part of Haig Road near Route Louri, were ordered by the French Concession Police to move out within two weeks. All circles have paid great attention to this. The 28th Branch of the Second District of this city has submitted a request to the Municipal Party Headquarters to find a way to rescue them. The text of their submission to the Party Headquarters of the Second District is recorded below: "Submitting a request. It is reported that about 200 households of thatched shed residents along the eastern part of Haig Road will be evicted by the French Concession Police and ordered to move out within two weeks and demolish the thatched sheds, and will not be allowed to live in the territory. It is shocking to read. It is found that the residents there are mostly Jiangbei rickshaw pullers, handcart pullers, coolie workers, and small business operators. They all fled to Shanghai to make a living because of the natural disasters and bandit disasters in Jiangbei over the years. Most of them came to Shanghai to escape the flood this time. Their struggling lives can be seen in general. Moreover, they have been living in thatched sheds there for many years. If they are driven away regardless, they will inevitably be displaced and unable to survive. In addition, the weather will gradually become colder in the future, and their suffering will be even more unpredictable. Our Party has always been concerned about liberating the suffering of the people, and should give them emergency rescue. It is difficult to stand by and watch thousands of compatriots being displaced and unable to survive. Therefore, we respectfully request your association to forward to the Municipal Party Headquarters and send a letter to the Municipal Government, requesting them to quickly build public housing in the West Shanghai area so that the Shanghai civilians can move in. And we also ask you to inform the French Concession authorities that they must not evict the civilians there before the public housing in West Shanghai is built. This matter concerns the suffering of the civilians, and it is reasonable to prepare a document and request your association to review and approve it. We will be very grateful. Respectfully presented to Luo Lie, Standing Committee Member of the 28th Branch of the Second District Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special City Committee of the Kuomintang, November 11."

Central Bank Inspection Report

▲ 107th Time

The 107th Inspection Report of the Central Bank's issuance reserve states: This council, according to Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the Bank's issuance of convertible banknotes. The 107th inspection was held on November 10th of the 20th year of the Republic of China at the Bank's Issuance Bureau. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 36,592,738 silver dollars, including: silver dollar notes totaling 33,872,325 silver dollars, and subsidiary currency notes totaling 2,720,413 silver dollars. Total amount of convertible banknote reserve: 36,592,738 silver dollars, including: cash reserve of 23,966,906 silver dollars. This cash reserve includes 18,312,359 silver dollars stored in the Bank's issuance vault, 1,997,042 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports, and 3,657,505 silver dollars deposited with other banks. Guarantee reserve, equivalent to 12,625,832 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknotes issued: 500,000 customs gold units. Total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknote reserve: 500,000 customs gold units. This reserve includes 200,000 US dollars deposited with other banks in this port, calculated at a fixed price of 0.40 for customs gold units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's regulations on convertible banknotes, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guarantee reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash exceeds 60%, and the guarantee is less than 40%. This is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. November 10th, 20th year of the Republic of China. Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fusun; Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilun.

Dispute Over Dismissal of Workers by the French Municipal Council's Engineering Department

▲ Originates from the Horse Racing Holiday Issue ▲ The Chinese Friendship Association Held a Meeting Yesterday

The New Shanghai Society reports that the French Concession Municipal Council has traditionally given a half-day holiday each year during the Western champagne races. On the 4th of this month, for the autumn racing season, the various departments of the Council still followed the old practice and stopped work in the afternoon. Peng Jinfu, the head foreman of the Council's Engineering Department, also asked the director for leave at noon. The director immediately stated that work would stop in the afternoon. Workers then returned home. Unexpectedly, the director issued a notice after the workers had left, stating that those who did not work this afternoon would be dismissed. Some workers living nearby heard the news and immediately returned to work. Those living further away received the news late. The next day, when the workers went to work, they were refused and announced the dismissal of 31 workers. The dismissed workers immediately reported to the Chinese Friendship Association, requesting assistance in restoring their jobs. Qiu Zhanggang, a standing committee member of the association, led the workers to negotiate with the director-general of the Council, Fan Erde (transliteration). As a result, they returned without success. Yesterday at 1:00 PM, the association convened an emergency meeting of all group leaders and general and deputy officers. More than 200 representatives attended. The city party headquarters also sent Zhou Funong to attend. Shen Caigeng presided over the meeting, and Zheng Fengchu recorded the minutes. After the opening formalities, the chairman first reported the meaning of the meeting's convocation. Subsequently, it was resolved that, in addition to requesting the city party headquarters to negotiate with the French authorities for the restoration of work, all workers should unite and help each other in the spirit of mutual assistance to seek the benefits to which they are entitled under the overall settlement conditions. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Dongmei Rescued from Abuse

An elderly woman surnamed Wu, residing in the west wing downstairs at No. 18, Lane 5, Ximen Road, French Concession, kept a maid named Dongmei, aged ten. Dongmei was often beaten with sticks and burned with fire by Wu, leaving scars all over her body. This matter came to the attention of the Chinese Children's Welfare Association. The association immediately sent Inspector Wang of the Protection Department, accompanied by Chinese detectives from the Loujiawan French police station, to investigate the matter. Unexpectedly, the old woman had taken Dongmei out, leaving only the wet nurse at home. They found no clues. When they reinvestigated the next day, the door was locked, and the whole family had fled. The inspector and the Chinese detectives, seeing that they had fled in fear of punishment, were certain that they had been abused. Just as they were about to return to the police station to arrest them closely, a righteous person named Wu Hongzhang, who claimed to know that the old woman abused the maid, said that if they could postpone the arrest for a day, he would find Dongmei and punish the person involved according to the severity of the injuries. The next afternoon at 4:00 PM, he brought the abused maid Dongmei to them. Inspector Wang and others carefully examined the girl's arms and face and found obvious burns and stick marks with many scars. They registered and photographed her and took her to the police station. After detailed examination and inquiry by Minister Bo of the Morality Department and translator Ren, it was determined that although the girl had no internal injuries, keeping maids was prohibited by national law. Therefore, they immediately ordered her to be handed over to the Children's Welfare Association for care. The person involved was treated leniently and not detained. The detectives were also instructed to prevent her from keeping maids again.

The Public Security Bureau Requests the Withdrawal of the Cooperation for the Summons of Lu Chengyao

Lu Chengyao, the general manager of the Wusong China Iron Factory, went to Liaoning to run another factory. News from Trade Associations

▲ Bean and Rice Industry: The rice measures required by the Bean and Rice Industry Association have always been manufactured by the Rengu Public Office. Members of the industry who need them must obtain them from the Public Office after they have been calibrated before they can be used. The standard has always been the Hai measure, which is no longer applicable. A new type of rice measure has been manufactured, with each measure being four dou and two sheng, and each shi being eight dou and four sheng. Five hundred have been manufactured and a resolution has been passed in a meeting to distribute them to each shop in the first month of the lunar calendar next year for practical use, and to abolish the old-fashioned Hai measures that are not applicable. The association believes that the new rice measure is different from the Hai measure, so it must be trained in advance to avoid disputes with boatmen after implementation. It is now scheduled to begin training on the 15th of this month. However, the measure clerks of each shop must report to the association for registration. The association is now notifying the north and south shops to inform the measure clerks to report for registration, limited to the 14th. Those who do not register will not be hired. The leaders of the rice industry groups are also notified to come to the meeting to supervise. It is said that this reform is very serious. If the clerks who are trained in the new measures are qualified, the shops may continue to hire them as usual. Therefore, the clerks who have been hired by the shops for two or three years are very alarmed. The clerks are discussing and requesting the association to postpone the registration and training. It is unknown whether this can be done.

▲ Rickshaw Industry: The Rickshaw Industry Association issued a notice yesterday for the establishment of a relief section, stating: "With all due respect, in recent years, during the floods in Jiangbei, rural rickshaw pullers have gathered in Shanghai. There are some unemployed vagrants who specialize in stealing vehicles and harming rickshaw pullers as their profession. The theft of cars for ransom has been seen for a long time, but recently it has become more and more serious, happening several times a day. It is unbearable to see. Although the police and government have repeatedly issued orders, strictly investigating and banning them, these thieves are incorrigible, disregarding the law, and dare to openly harm the business of car dealers and harm rickshaw pullers, which is very infuriating. Therefore, the Executive Committee of this association resolved on November 10 that, in order to prevent car theft, we should unite actively. All those with more than 500 rickshaws can automatically form a group and hold a no-ransom doctrine. We deeply hope that everyone will have the spirit of unyielding righteousness and never redeem the car, so as to consistently eliminate the phenomenon of car theft, then the future of our car industry is full of hope. With all due respect, I would like to express my views. Enclosed is a brief regulation on the Relief Section of the Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Association. Article 1: This section is organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 5, Paragraph 3 of the Articles of Association of this Association. Article 2: The purpose of this section is to gather the strength of the group, prevent car theft and ransom, and increase the welfare of car dealers and rickshaw pullers, and everyone should hold the doctrine of no redemption. Article 3: Vehicles in this city can automatically gather five vehicles and automatically form a group. A group may nominate five to seven managers and elect a group leader. The group leader may participate in handling the overall relief affairs of the section. Article 4: The powers of each group's office are to investigate and handle the daily affairs of the group, and compensate for car losses, etc. All external documents, publicity, etc., are handled by the association. Article 5: If a vehicle is stolen, the group leader shall report it to the section, and the section shall forward it to the association to request the competent authority to pay attention to the investigation and publish it in the newspaper. Article 6: The section shall have two directors, who shall be nominated by the Executive Committee of the association from the executive committee members, and shall jointly handle the daily relief affairs with the standing committee members of the association and the group leaders. Article 7: The car compensation method is divided into the following five items: (1) If a vehicle is stolen, regardless of whether it is new or old, each vehicle in the group shall pay five-sixths of the compensation, and the rickshaw puller shall pay one-sixth of the compensation, and a new car shall be purchased for business. If it is insufficient, the car owner shall supplement it. (2) If the car is stolen from the car owner's home, it shall be handled automatically by each group. If the rickshaw puller runs away (commonly known as 'stealing the car'), it is the car owner's improper employment and is not an example of compensation. (3) After the vehicle is stolen, the responsible persons of each organization shall be immediately informed of the process, and then the group leader shall report it to the section for record, and send a letter to each district office and the competent authority to pay attention to the investigation and pay attention to the traces of the vehicle. (4) After the vehicle is compensated, and the original vehicle is found, if rubber pads and other accessories are lost, they shall be compensated according to the new ones, otherwise, a reasonable amount of car rental loss shall be given, but the amount of compensation that has been paid shall be refunded in full. (5) If the car owner and the rickshaw puller collude to deceive the same industry and privately redeem the car, once the investigation is verified, the association shall request the competent authority to deal with it according to law and revoke its license plate as a warning. Article 8: The daily expenses of this section (such as paper, pens, etc.) shall be borne by the association. Article 9: The car compensation funds of each group shall be collected by each group's own deliberation. However, at the end of each month, each group must report the economic income and expenditure and the number of car compensation and lost cars to the section for statistical registration. Article 10: This brief regulation shall be implemented after being approved by the Executive Committee of the Association. Article 11: If there are any matters not covered in this brief regulation, the Executive Committee of the Association shall amend it."

News from Various Trade Unions

▲ The Lead Printing Industry Union held a joint meeting of the directors and supervisors the day before yesterday, chaired by Tao Dechang. After the opening formalities, the following motions were discussed: (1) The case of how the union should deal with the dismissal of workers by the capitalists at the Zhenxing branch office. It was resolved to send Wang Xingquan to negotiate. (2) The case of how to deal with the apprentice Guan Yu, who stopped working due to the inability to improve his treatment, and is temporarily staying in the union. It was resolved to copy each person's address clearly, and in addition to introducing them to work, give them travel expenses to return. If the journey is long, they will stay in the union temporarily. (3) New members of the union who joined within November, in addition to the membership fee, should pay three months of union fees, and those who joined after November should pay one and a half yuan in union fees. Resolved: passed. (4) The case of the entire workforce of the Zhonghe Guanglu Printing Bureau requesting to join the union. Resolved: Handed over to the Board of Supervisors for review. (5) After November 1st, the union's accounting department will be completely independent and will be responsible for by Chen Zuwang. Before November 1st, Liang Yuling will be responsible for the handover. In addition, the union will give Comrade Chen a travel allowance of four yuan. Resolved: In addition to the original case being passed, all foreign offices will be notified to check accordingly. (6) Send a letter to the Yuankang branch office to urge the members who have not paid the fund to pay it off. Resolved: passed. (7) The income and expenditure accounts of the accounting department must be announced to all the firms before the 5th of each month. Resolved: passed. (8) Secret. (9) Secret. (10) How should the union express its opinion on the heroic resistance to Japan by Chairman Ma of Heilongjiang Province? Resolved: Send a telegram of condolences: "General Ma of Longjiang and all the soldiers and civilians, the Japanese slaves are showing their fierce Jiangnan, Fortunately, our Heilongjiang Province soldiers have fought bravely, finally causing the thieves' flames to be damaged and the enemy's courage to be chilled. All of our people can be impressed. We send a telegram of condolences and hope to continue our efforts." (11) Adjournment

▲ The Sixth District Cotton Weaving Industry Union held its second joint meeting of directors and supervisors and a temporary representative meeting the day before yesterday, chaired by Wu Biyu. After the chairman's report, the discussion began immediately. (1) The case of the workers of the Dafeng Factory requesting to resume work. Resolved: Gu Yuchen will still assist the new standing committee to handle the reinstatement of all the dismissed workers of the factory. (2) Worker No. 204 has died of illness (originally borrowed 23 yuan per month from the Zhenhua factory, including meals). He had found a representative to replace the work. Now, it is forbidden for the representative to resume work when the repayment is due. Resolved: The union will send someone to investigate and handle the matter. (3) Election of the new standing committee. Resolved: Wu Biyu, Zhong Xiaobao. (4) Request that the new standing committee Wu Biyu's machine position be given to the old standing committee Gu Yuchen. Resolved: Passed. (5) Employing Wang Guoliang as a secretary. Resolved: Passed.

▲ The First Branch of the Ship Timber Industry Union held a joint meeting of the branch's directors and the Security Committee yesterday, chaired by Fang Ronggeng and recorded by Zhou Rui. After the opening formalities, the chairman gave an opening speech. The following items were discussed: (1) Regarding the employment of workers in the industry, both the foreman and the worker should be considered, and the overall goal should be to maintain the development and scope of the business. Resolved: Hereafter, the foremen will employ workers at the former public office as the general mechanism, and they will no longer be allowed to directly employ workers elsewhere. (2) When a worker loses his job, he must not directly ask the foreman to work, but must first go to the former public office to register, and then be hired in order. (3) If the Yidaijiao and Nanshi areas are far away, and it is inconvenient to register and hire, it is stipulated that the Lingnan Building and Zhabei Renhe Building teahouses in Nanshi should be notified by the former public office to hire. (4) If the foreman hires a worker without calling for employment at the public office, the private direct employment will be invalid. (5) If an unreasonable dispute occurs between the foreman and the worker, the responsible person of the union shall be responsible for mediation between the two parties. (6) If other factories or companies employ non-members for work within the scope of the industry, each worker shall report to the person in charge of the union to persuade or negotiate with the company, and order them to withdraw non-members, so as to employ the industry's workers. (7) (Secret) (8) If the foreman privately employs non-members, he will be severely punished once discovered. (9) (10) (Secret) (11) The above-mentioned cases are of great importance to the livelihood and business of the industry. They should be reported to the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for approval, and then a date will be set for the meeting to implement the measures. Other cases were omitted.

▲ The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of the Cloth Industry Workers held its third preparatory meeting the day before yesterday, with 160 preparatory members and representatives from various stores attending. Resolved: (A) How should the second step of soliciting members of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association be carried out? Resolved: (1) Send a copy of the letter to the managers and workers of each store. (2) Each preparatory member should start soliciting on the 13th. (3) Recommend Chen Guoliang and others to assist the preparatory members in soliciting. (B) Should the date of establishment be changed due to the rush to complete the procedures? Resolved: Changed to 7:00 PM on the 16th at No. North Shunzhen Lane, Huaxing Road, to hold the founding meeting. (C) The charter has been drafted. Please review it. Resolved: Handed over to the original drafter to fill in the review and submit it to the General Assembly for discussion. (D) Should the four preparatory members who did not attend the second meeting be removed? Resolved: Temporarily retained.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory’s weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong and the Yangtze River basin, as well as coastal areas, would be cloudy with rain or fog in some places. There would be a northeasterly wind in the East China Sea and an undefined wind in the Yellow Sea. The weather south of the Taiwan Strait and along the coast of Guangdong would be extremely bad. The center of a hurricane was located at approximately 6:00 AM, one within 60 miles of the intersection of 20 degrees north latitude and 116 degrees east longitude, moving northwestward; and another within 120 miles of the intersection of 11 degrees north latitude and 142 degrees east longitude, moving northwest-westward. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 61.2 degrees and the lowest was 56.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 55.6 degrees and the lowest was 44.8 degrees.

Letter to the Editor

To the esteemed Editor,

In the local news column of your newspaper on the 9th of this month, there was a news item about the petition to the peace representatives by the labor union representatives of this city. Among them were the names “National Medicine Labor Union” and “National Medicine Industry Workers Union.” Upon investigation, the only trade union for national medicine workers in this city, apart from the dissolved (Shanghai Pharmaceutical Industry Workers Union), has no other name. It is suspected that there was an error in your newspaper’s reporting. Therefore, this letter is specially prepared for clarification and correction. We sincerely request that this letter be published in the “Letters to the Editor” column.

Respectfully,

To the Editor of Shen Bao,

Shanghai Pharmaceutical Industry Workers Union.

Reader Correspondence

Mr. Zhu Daquan’s News (Omitted)

(National Products Should Not Increase in Price Amidst the Strong Anti-Japanese Resistance)

(Answer) At this time when the whole country is unanimously boycotting Japanese goods, it is indeed hateful for domestic product manufacturers or merchants to take advantage of the opportunity to temporarily raise the prices of domestic goods. If this is the case, they should ask themselves if their conscience feels uneasy. However, a distinction must be made. Domestic product manufacturers also have their own unspeakable difficulties. China’s manufacturing experience is not as extensive as that of foreign countries, management is not as scientific as that of foreign countries, production and sales are not as wide as those of foreign countries, and government assistance to industrialists is not as strong as that of foreign countries. Therefore, it is indeed extremely difficult to demand that the price of domestic goods be lower than that of foreign goods in this immature stage. We on the social side must also forgive them for this. However, if the original price of a domestic product was not so high and it is suddenly raised temporarily, then that is absolutely unacceptable. Patriotic industrialists and merchants should definitely not do this.

Book Review

Introducing "To the Youth"

— Qi Ren

Recently, it has been truly difficult to find reading material that directly guides young people. It's not that there is nothing for young people to read. In recent years, since the wave of the New Literature movement has risen, the quantity of magazines and publications, to say the least, has been astonishing. But in terms of quality, they only indirectly guide young people by citing examples, and rarely contribute their own experiences to young people. Therefore, what young people gain is at most just an image in their minds, thinking that this is a "category."

Although, I have found a few books after all. Zhu Guangqian's "Twelve Letters to Young People" and Shu Xincheng's "Letter to Young People" both have decent content. Here, I have found a third book, Xia Ruimin's "To the Youth," which I will enthusiastically introduce to you respectable and beloved young people.

The author is someone who has just passed through the "youth" stage and is about to step into "adulthood." He has experienced the beautiful youth that ordinary people go through, and he hasn't completely left it yet. He has an image in his mind that won't be lost immediately, and he has released it and written this book.

Therefore, this book will be more substantial than "Twelve Letters to Young People" and more intimate than "Letter to Young People."

The author is a genuine and courageous young man. He says, "I simply do not acknowledge the existence of so-called geniuses or intelligent people in this world. They are made that way by their environment. I believe that the acquisition of experience is the only 'correctness' that does not deceive. I advise young people not to hope to become 'supermen,' but rather to be serious and down-to-earth." When this national crisis is upon us and ordinary bewildered young people are still at a loss, this book is enough to make them feel excited, and at least it can point them to a correct path to take.

People are absolutely dominated by their environment and history. What kind of era produces what kind of youth. The author cannot escape this scope, so he has also enjoyed pleasure, suffered hardship, and experienced all kinds of things. He wants to leave these things for those who come later to see, to write down what he has truly personally experienced, as a historical record of a young person in a certain era. So he says,

"Looking back, when I was young, I also talked grandly about studies, pursued love, participated in various sports, liked to show off, and wanted to become a writer. In short, what ordinary young people tacitly hope for, I could not escape this scope either. Recently, I really want to leave a trace of the path I have walked, as a memorial to myself. The next biggest reason is that I want to reverently contribute to the modern lovable youth, as a first meeting gift, because these are my fragmented personal insights. I dare not exaggerate in any way, I can only say that they are some records of my youth journey, a faithful plea to modern youth." Therefore, we know how the author wants to offer his sincere heart.

The characteristic of this book is that it shows the author passing through the "bridge of youth" amidst difficulties and hardships, with various harsh environments tempting him. The fragile heart of youth cannot easily avoid these demons. Therefore, the author has also personally tasted these things. But precisely because the environment is making him fall, it is all the more sufficient to forge his strong spirit. The environment is making him fall everywhere, but his indomitable will confronts it everywhere. When he was living through his youth, he didn't feel anything, but when he got older, he felt that he had crossed many dangerous bridges. Thinking back, it makes him feel chilled. So the purpose of writing this book is to tell young people, what kind of road is placed in front of you, and how you will have to be careful to deal with it. So he says, "...and now there are many young people groping in the dark, and perhaps it is not without benefit to look at the records of these pioneers (one who groped in the dark before you)."

Therefore, this book is still an autobiography of youth. The author painstakingly offers what he has personally experienced to younger youth, so that they can see what kind of road the pioneers have taken, what kind of situation they have encountered, and then perhaps they can walk more steadily and practically on their own journey.

The author also deeply understands the current generation of young people's boredom with the times. Therefore, he also uses an encouraging tone to lead young people onto the right path. He says,

"The waves of the times are constantly stirring up huge tides, causing each and every young person to be confused and walk towards the ivory tower or the intersection of the crossroads. But we must not listen to other people's declarations and be bewildered and at a loss. We can only fulfill our own responsibilities, hold on to the times, and move forward..."

This book especially emphasizes young literary people. The author sees that they like literature, which is of course gratifying, but it is quite dangerous for some people to like to create at every turn. So he says,

"Literature is ultimately an art. What it needs is generally fluent writing and trained writing, and especially what it needs is the life, passion, and genius of general art. The cultivation of this passion and genius requires real literary cultivation..."

The diction of this book is also very beautiful, making people feel quite happy to read it. He always uses some elegant sentences to adjust in each chapter.

"Jianfu, the weather is very warm today, and the small river flows down from the hillside with rippling shallow waves, shining in the sunlight. The campus is covered with the tender green of early spring, and rose trees and poplar trees are blooming and growing. The tender leaves are slightly green, and there are small birds singing everywhere. A spring atmosphere arises in the rural air, and infinite joy shines on the silent space. All energy is about to grow from the earth." Also,

"...Outside, the flowing water and the clear sound of the spring vibrate my soul, thus making me remember you..."

In short, │This book is a pure and sincere expression of the heart of a young person, and it becomes an experienced guide, which cannot be compared with general empty discussions.

Finally, I will end with the author's words:

"When you know that spring has come, especially do not forget that you are a young person, and you should work doubly hard in your youth. I advise you to put down a glass of fine wine in your left hand and raise your right hand to proceed, proceed."

Shanghai Market

Business News

▲Youlian Film Company declares that the "Female Knight-Errant of the Wild River" film produced by this company and written by Gu Mingdao is famous at home and abroad, and known to women and children. Now the eighth episode has been completed, and the program is "Breaking the Snail Valley." The content is lively, with thrilling tension, unprecedented stunts in fierce battles, hilarious comedy interludes, and bizarre plots of giant bandits robbing money. It will be released at the Central Grand Theater starting on the 14th of this month. It is a must-see, and so on.

▲Guohuo Huali Brand Cigarettes declares that the 20-pack Huali brand cigarettes of this company are produced by the China Zhonghe Tobacco Company in this port. Now, at a time when anti-Japanese fervor is high, they have been mistakenly identified as enemy goods. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, in order to protect domestic goods, specially telegraphed to Xiamen yesterday, saying: "To the Anti-Japanese Association of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: The Huali brand cigarettes produced by the Zhonghe Tobacco Company in this city are indeed domestic goods. This is specially telegraphed for verification. Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Yangyin."

▲Jinghua Company, Baoxing Road, London Road, Zhabei, declares that this company is a flower paper factory for making various porcelain and enamelware, exclusively run by Chinese people. It can also be used on metal and woodware. The results are better than those of enemy goods, and the price is as low as one-quarter of theirs.

▲Yulun Silk and Satin Shop on Nanjing Road declares that the owner of this shop recently went to famous factories in various parts of the country to supervise the manufacture of a large batch of durable and beautiful seasonal clothing materials, such as Zhongshan satin, brocade satin, and factory crepe, wild goose bell crepe, and other goods. All kinds are original and can be called the best of domestic goods. In order to promote domestic goods, the price is specially low, which is even more different from imported goods.
